                              CREATE PUBLIC SYNONYM prod_dw.STATE_APPROVAL_INFO FOR PROD_DW.STATE_APPROVAL_INFO 
                              CREATE PUBLIC SYNONYM prod_dw.ST_APPR_INF_TO_BOARD_CERT_INF FOR PROD_DW.ST_APPR_INF_TO_BOARD_CERT_INF
                              CREATE PUBLIC SYNONYM prod_dw.BOARD_CERTIFICATION_INFO FOR PROD_DW.BOARD_CERTIFICATION_INFO 
                              CREATE PUBLIC SYNONYM prod_dw.board_appr_speciality_code FOR PROD_DW.board_appr_speciality_code 
                              CREATE PUBLIC SYNONYM prod_dw.ACCUMLTD_VAL_TOTAL_FACT FOR PROD_DW.ACCUMLTD_VAL_TOTAL_FACT 
                              CREATE PUBLIC SYNONYM prod_dw.MEMBER_PLAN_SEL_HIST_FACT FOR PROD_DW.MEMBER_PLAN_SEL_HIST_FACT
